Bitcoin master branch sync log
==============================

- "v" means commit was merged;
- "cr" means commit was merged after resolving conflicts;
- "pr" means commit is merge commit (usually a pull request merge) and was skipped;
- "s" means commit was skipped for a reason specified
- "ff" means fatal failure
